          &lt;div class="date-outer"&gt;
        
&lt;h2 class='date-header'&gt;&lt;span&gt;Sunday, July 10, 2011&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;

          &lt;div class="date-posts"&gt;
        
&lt;div class='post-outer'&gt;
&lt;div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'&gt;
&lt;meta content='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-yO5V4L4uZ6A/Thn_gSgASdI/AAAAAAAABoY/O7ufy9dClyc/s320/IMG_0510.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='7356703545551301104' itemprop='blogId'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='7533561126041817745' itemprop='postId'/&gt;
&lt;a name='7533561126041817745'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
I gave in.
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7533561126041817745' itemprop='description articleBody'&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
Ok, I gave in and actually &lt;i&gt;did&lt;/i&gt; a DIY project and I really committed to it. Kind of. &nbsp;What did I get myself into?&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Everyone has been pinning on &lt;span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: #cc0000;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://pinterest.com/"&gt;Pinterest&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt; {I first saw it &lt;span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: #cc0000;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://fantasticinfirst.blogspot.com/2011/02/crate-solution.html"&gt;*here*&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;} like CRAZY this wonderful storage seating idea with &lt;span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: #e06666; font-size: large;"&gt;crates&lt;/span&gt;. &nbsp;Well...I jumped into it and thought I'd do it! &lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;P.S. They are pretty low to the ground {for 1st graders} when you put them at your guided reading table. I just lowered my table a little bit and I think it'll work just fine!&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-bottom: 0.5em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; padding-bottom: 6px; padding-left: 6px; padding-right: 6px; padding-top: 6px; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-yO5V4L4uZ6A/Thn_gSgASdI/AAAAAAAABoY/O7ufy9dClyc/s1600/IMG_0510.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" height="240" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-yO5V4L4uZ6A/Thn_gSgASdI/AAAAAAAABoY/O7ufy9dClyc/s320/IMG_0510.JPG" style="cursor: move;" width="320" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class="tr-caption" style="font-size: 13px; padding-top: 4px; text-align: center;"&gt;The finished product!&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
Before you freak out when you see how much I spent, please be aware that I wanted to just get this project finished. I didn't take my time to price it out or &lt;i&gt;&lt;span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;"&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;b&gt;seek donations&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;. &nbsp;I'm pretty sure Wal-Mart &nbsp;and Home Depot would have donated most of the items used {if I would have been patient in getting those items}.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Remember I made 6 crate seats! You can start small!&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: left;"&gt;
&lt;span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;"&gt;&lt;b&gt;Supplies and expected costs for&lt;u&gt; 6 crates:&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Staple Gun {16.43- Home Depot}&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Staples 8mm {2.67- Home Depot}&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;(2) 1/2 inch thick plywood about 2'X4' {22.52 for 2 - Home Depot}&nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Cutting the wood to fit in the crate {Free- Home Depot}&nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;(6) Crates {20.82 for 6- Wal-Mart}&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Spray Glue {5.97- Wal-Mart}&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;(2) Foam Roll 1 inch thick {32.00- Wal-Mart...*ouch*, instead of buying this foam I bought, just buy the egg shell foam mats!}&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Ribbon {1.97- Wal-mart}&nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fabric {3.5 yards at $15.94-Wal-Mart}&nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;A husband willing to help you out {PRICELESS!}&nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: left;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: x-large;"&gt;Here is my tutorial!&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: x-large;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-qFPUb6g0GrI/ThoAWgB1hWI/AAAAAAAABog/k6UTZuQqz-Y/s1600/IMG_0497.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" height="240" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-qFPUb6g0GrI/ThoAWgB1hWI/AAAAAAAABog/k6UTZuQqz-Y/s320/IMG_0497.JPG" width="320" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"&gt;After having the Home Depot worker cut my pieces my hubby had to take them home and sand the corners down to round them out.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-4hqgiIsk1yA/ThoAbMHbprI/AAAAAAAABok/hi0IjxJ4Ams/s1600/IMG_0498.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" height="240" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-4hqgiIsk1yA/ThoAbMHbprI/AAAAAAAABok/hi0IjxJ4Ams/s320/IMG_0498.JPG" width="320" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"&gt;Cut the foam to fit on the wood.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-YwlbyYlXM5A/ThoAgGOL1NI/AAAAAAAABoo/wPPK3x935ek/s1600/IMG_0499.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" height="240" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-YwlbyYlXM5A/ThoAgGOL1NI/AAAAAAAABoo/wPPK3x935ek/s320/IMG_0499.JPG" width="320" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"&gt;Use spray adhesive on the wood focusing on the edges. &nbsp;Pat down the fabric to ensure it sticks all around. Let dry for 2 hours.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-r6T0HjXmgNk/Thn-meaX8CI/AAAAAAAABn4/9kZ8cOUE3JI/s1600/IMG_0500.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" height="240" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-r6T0HjXmgNk/Thn-meaX8CI/AAAAAAAABn4/9kZ8cOUE3JI/s320/IMG_0500.JPG" width="320" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"&gt;Cut the fabric&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-BfvOrJrHuOo/Thn-8s_f3zI/AAAAAAAABoE/j1mm2fJfPDU/s1600/IMG_0505.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" height="320" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-BfvOrJrHuOo/Thn-8s_f3zI/AAAAAAAABoE/j1mm2fJfPDU/s320/IMG_0505.JPG" width="240" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"&gt;It's best to have someone help you staple. I pulled the fabric tight and my husband used his muscles to staple.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-jRYJFj6DIYk/Thn-stiuW5I/AAAAAAAABn8/_c_G3PbP-Dc/s1600/IMG_0503.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" height="240" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-jRYJFj6DIYk/Thn-stiuW5I/AAAAAAAABn8/_c_G3PbP-Dc/s320/IMG_0503.JPG" width="320" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"&gt;The corners look much like a present being wrapped.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-w5Cbj8b9W8A/Thn_GXXU9gI/AAAAAAAABoI/VonQ62Q2dPM/s1600/IMG_0506.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" height="320" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-w5Cbj8b9W8A/Thn_GXXU9gI/AAAAAAAABoI/VonQ62Q2dPM/s320/IMG_0506.JPG" width="240" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"&gt;Fit your ribbon {for the handle} and place in the middle.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vaDzNcs6F1g/Thn_M3lSzDI/AAAAAAAABoM/CcbavhrTvYk/s1600/IMG_0507.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" height="240" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vaDzNcs6F1g/Thn_M3lSzDI/AAAAAAAABoM/CcbavhrTvYk/s320/IMG_0507.JPG" width="320" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"&gt;Pull the ribbon tight (but not too tight) and start stapling!&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-8LaC2XxLOpg/Thn_ZOw319I/AAAAAAAABoU/NXjkMeD1hyM/s1600/IMG_0509.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" height="240" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-8LaC2XxLOpg/Thn_ZOw319I/AAAAAAAABoU/NXjkMeD1hyM/s320/IMG_0509.JPG" width="320" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"&gt;You can use the ribbon as a handle to pull the seat out so you can store items in your crate.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-yO5V4L4uZ6A/Thn_gSgASdI/AAAAAAAABoY/O7ufy9dClyc/s1600/IMG_0510.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" height="240" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-yO5V4L4uZ6A/Thn_gSgASdI/AAAAAAAABoY/O7ufy9dClyc/s320/IMG_0510.JPG" width="320" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"&gt;The finished product! &lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
My kiddos LOVE the crate seats during guided reading!&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OeTTeYh6Z2g/Tk2RTIRCbPI/AAAAAAAAByo/aGPqa8mOitE/s1600/IMG_0540.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" height="300" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OeTTeYh6Z2g/Tk2RTIRCbPI/AAAAAAAAByo/aGPqa8mOitE/s400/IMG_0540.JPG" width="400" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: purple; font-size: large;"&gt;&lt;b&gt;OK LISTEN UP&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;! &nbsp;I did not expect it to be &lt;span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: x-large;"&gt;this much&lt;/span&gt; of a project. I was &lt;span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: x-small;"&gt;thisclose&lt;/span&gt; to quitting because I get frustrated with DIY projects way too soon. I think if Home Depot could have cut off the corners for us, we wouldn't have spend 1+ hours sanding them down. &nbsp;Make sure you take your crate in when you get the wood cut. &nbsp;Don't just measure! &lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
As you can see we've only finished one. I felt so accomplished that I posted this before all of them were finished. :) &nbsp;Maybe I'll update this post with all of them together {I bought a different piece of fabric for all of them!}.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
If you'd like a printable version of the tutorial click &lt;span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: #cc0000; font-size: large;"&gt;&lt;a href="https://docs.google.com/viewer?a=v&amp;pid=explorer&amp;chrome=true&amp;srcid=0B1Nqou3fOm91OGExZTZiN2ItMDkwNy00YWE4LWI4ZWMtMzMxMmQzNDFhYzc5&amp;hl=en_US"&gt;*HERE*&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;Great tips from our readers:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
*Instead of buying the foam from the craft department, but the egg shell foam pads in the bed/bath department- It will be much cheaper!&lt;br /&gt;
*Try your local grocery store to get donated crates {eggs/milk are delivered in them!}&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

&lt;dd class='comment-body' id='Blog1_cmt-1465303295286691936'&gt;
&lt;p&gt;
I made these for my classroom last summer and love them!  The students really like sitting on them, and I love the storage!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Hints:  My husband cut the corners with a saw.  We didn&#39;t sand them.  Instead of the roll of foam, I bought one of the foam things for mattresses ($10 at Walmart).  It wasn&#39;t smooth like the roll but that didn&#39;t matter once they were put together.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;It was a family project at our house.  My daughter had a great time helping with these and is making 3 of them to take to college with her this fall!
&lt;/p&gt;
